This contract proposal is based on the understanding that apple growth is stimulated when there are more apples close by. By discouraging consumption in low-density regions, we can ensure that apples are left to grow and multiply. This will not only increase the total number of apples available but also distribute them more evenly across the grid, making it easier for all players to collect apples. The punishment of transferring 1 apple to the other players who agree to use contracting is a fair penalty that will further discourage overconsumption.
